			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of municipalities in Germany</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p><b>List of <a href="/wiki/Municipalities_of_Germany" title="Municipalities of Germany">municipalities in Germany</a></b> with over 10,000 inhabitants in the year 2000. The list is sorted by population and gives the <a href="/wiki/States_of_Germany" title="States of Germany">state</a> of every municipality. Where the German name differs from the English, it is given in parentheses.</p>
